0(): ga na nag zhagan/
1(): rdza rba da zag pa brgyad na 'das tha thags pa
1a1(1): bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa thams cad kyi snying po rig pa 'dzin pa'i sde snod rdo rje theg pa snga 'gyur
1a2(1): rgyud 'bum rin po che'i rtogs pa brjod pa lha'i rnga bo che lta bu'i gtam zhes bya ba'i stod cha bzhugs so//
1b1(1): rgyu d+hA rgya ba thong sa pa mnyams ga sum nu brgyu gas kyi kyi za gnanapar rar ra mi rdzun panas nyis pa sa rgyan tho ma pa na ma// pa rgyu
1b2(1): 'a somal rlom mi seMs ma mnam zi las sa seM oM nA~M hoH/
1b3(1): khor rab de ma hA mu badz+ra ye tA k+SharaM shA shwat+tha dau rni ra d+hi Sh+Ta sa skr-i N+yaid+hU to shama?
1b4(1): @##/ mi 'gyur rtag brtan gdod ma'i 'gog bden 'dus ma byas dbyings gang du rab zhi rdul bral ye shes bde ba chen po thugs chud pas//
1b5(1): / slangam lho/ mtha mon can rgyu /
2a1(1): thos ga sa mas ma
2a2(1): b+hu ba na sha mi ta yo&s+t+ri tA tsin+tu pUr+N+NaM gu NaM r+d+har+m+ma/ rA dz+ya shri yA ni t+ya sam+bad+ba b+hA be dza ga tra/
2a3(1): srid zhi'i khams su mi gnas bsam gyis mi khyab mtha' dag yon tan chos kyi rgyal srid dpal gyis rtag tu 'byor pa nyid gyur cing //
2b1(1): gan
2b2(1): gagasamam man ma can mams sa rgyams mama'am ma man rmi
3a1(1): ma rnam sa tshigagasanas/ gagonams// gams/ mam gyigag / na
3a2(1): rab 'byams rgya mtsho'i bde bar gshegs pa'i mi mnyam mnyam pa med pa'i sku gsum tshul la mchog tu dad pas phyag 'tshal lo// //
3b1(1): sna tshogs spros pa rnams kyis ma spros brtag par mi nus shes bya kun la ro mnyam gyur pa gdod nas rab zhi'i dbyings de dang // rtog bral so so rang gi rig pas chos kun de nyid yul dang yul can
3b2(1): gnyis su med gzigs ji lta ji snyed mkhyen tshul can// gang la dmigs pa spangs pa nyid kyis 'du byas khams su nyams par mi 'gyur rtogs pa dam pa chos mchog gzhan du mi g.yo ba//
3b3(1): de der bkri byed ngo bo rgyu rkyen 'brel par bcas pa'i rjod byed nyid gyur lung gi chos la'ang rtag tu gus pas rim gro bgyi// rang bzhin mi 'khrugs za ba zhi spos bral 'od gsal khams su gnyis
3b4(1): snang blo yis dri ma rab bsags glo bur dang ldan 'khor ba'i chos// rab rib tshogs dang mngon par mtshungs pa'i kun nas sgrib byed thabs mkhas chen po'i mig sman bsten pas rim pa bzhin
3b5(1): du rab sbyangs pas// dkar po'i phyogs kyi cha shas ji bzhin phyogs mtshon tsam nas mtha' dag yon tan kun tu rdzogs par rim pa nyid kyis mngon snang ba'i// gnas lugs bden pa
3b6(1): gzigs tshul nyid kyis rim par phye ba theg gsum 'phags pa phyogs su bslan bcas dge 'dun la yang gus pas 'dud// zad dang mi skye'i ye shes pas brtag dka'i yon tan pha mtha' mi
4a1(1): mngon de lan 'ang // sangs rgyas gsang gi sgra dbyang sa chos kyi 'khar ma nyid yang nges 'ag thob dpan gzugs kyis dang // zhi ba'i dbyings su rtag par man
4a2(1): la lar 'bar dpal lar de bzhin chags tshul gyis// spyod tshul gcig pa'i mthar mi gnas pas sems can khams gzung grub pa mchog brnyes rnams la 'dud// sems can rnams la
4a3(1): mdza' ba nyid gyur bsgrub bya gang yin dam bca'i ri mo snying bkod nas// rab tu 'bad pa du ma'i ba dan g.yo ba gzhig par rab dka' snying stobs chen po'i gzings// zab cing rgya che byang chub
4a4(1): spyod pa'i chu gter cher zhugs gang gis thob pas gtan bde yi// 'dod brdo'i gzhir mur rgyal bstan rin chen 'dren pa'i ded dpon gang yin de la snying nas 'dud// grags pa'i me tog
4a5(1): 'dzum pa'i gter gyur legs byas brgya yi 'bras bus bdag nyid 'byor pa na// srid pa gsum gyi zug rngu gzhil ba'i chos mchog sman chen bsod nams zong du nyer khugs pas// spang dang
4a6(1): klog pa'i lam chen gyis phye thub bstan snang bas lha ngan la dga' kun+da'i tshal// cig car zum byed chos ldan rgyal po chos bzhin mdzad rnams rnam thar dran pas dang phyag brtsegs//
4b1(1): gang yang gdod nas gzhan don la goms snying rje chen pos lcags kyu'i dbang gyur glang po bzhin// ma lus 'gro rgyud chos la 'bab phyir legs gsung snang ba bla na med sbyin srid pa 'dir//
4b2(1): snyigs ma'i skyon gyis bag la zha ba'i drang srong chen po'i ring lugs slar yang slong byed pas// 'jig rten gsum gyi mchod sdong nyid gyur tshad ma'i skyes bu de la dad pa'i 'dab brgya grol//
4b3(1): gang zhig don dam ngo bo yul dang yon tan la gnas de yi rang bzhin dag gyur pas// khams dang phung po'i chos las rab brgal gang du shes min spros pa rnams kyi mthar ma lhungs//
4b4(1): dngos dang dngos med gnyi ga ro mnyam shes rab dbyings su bde chen sku ni khyab cing rtag/ chos la rmongs pa'i kun rtog mun bral mi mnyam 'bras ster sngags kyi theg pa mchog tu bstan
4b5(1): gzhal bar dka' ba'i rin chen zong gis rab 'byams rgya mtsho'i 'jig rten nyul yang thob dka' ba'i// thub mchog bstan pa yongs kyi dbus gnas thun mongs/ smin grub pa'i skyes
4b6(1): bus bsten gyur las// cha shas tsam zhig byang phyogs 'dir snang mi yi bdag pos rgya chen legs byas 'du bgyis te// skye bo'i tshogs la bdud rtsi'i bgo skal mi 'dzad bkye
5a1(1): / ba'i ngo mtshar gang zhig 'dir brjod pa// de la bde bar gshegs pa'i bstan pa thams cad kyi snying po gsang chen blan med pa de rje theg pa'i rgyud rje rin po che 'di
5a2(1): thog mar gang gis bstan pa'i ston pa dang des ji ltar gsungs pa'i tshul de dag gnas yul so sor ji ltar bab cing 'phel ba'i tshul// de las phyi mo'i tshogs ji snyed pa bar du bsgrubs pa dang /
5a3(1): glegs bam so sor ji ltar bzhugs pa'i rnam grangs/ legs spyad don ldan du bya ba'i shis brjod dang bsngo smon gyis mtha' brgyan pa bcas skabs lnga rim pa bzhin du gleng bar bya'o//
5a4(1): dang po la'ang gsum ste/ gdod ma'i mgon po chos kyi skur mngon par byang chub tshul/ de'i rnam 'phrul rdo rje 'chang gis zhing 'dir zhi ba brnyes tshul/ de las gzugs sku gnyis
5a5(1): kyi sprul pa sdang tshul su dang ye shes kyi khyad par dang bcas pa 'chad pa la/ spyir theg dman rnams kyi 'dod par/ 'o sol gyi ston pa 'di lta bur yang / so so skye bo grangs med
5a6(1): gsum du thar pa cha mthun bsags pa zhig srid pa tha ma par gyur pa byang chub snying po rdo rje'i gdan du srod la bdud btul/ gung la bsam gtan bzhi'i dngos gzhis sbyor lam rgyud la
5b1(1): bskyed nas/ tho rangs skya rengs 'char ka'i skad cig gcig la pha rol tu phyin pa drug mngon du mdzad nas chos dang gzugs su'i bdag nyid can du sangs rgyas te/ kun shes nas rab
5b2(1): bzang gi bar chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba sogs las sku gsum gyi rnam gzhag tshang bar khas mi len la/ theg chen gyi mdo sde rnams su gsungs pa'i sku gsum dang / sngags
5b3(1): la'ang byi nang gi mngon byang lnga dang / rgyu 'bras rdo rje 'dzin pa/ lus rtsa sbrul sru/ yid longs su/ khams bdud rtsi chos kyi sku/ snying po ye shes rlung ngo bo nyid
5b4(1): kyi sku sogs gdul bya dbang po rno rtul dang lam pa'i rnal 'byor pa'i mos pa'i dbang gis de ltar bstan pa tsam du zad la/ re zhig theg mchog bla na med pa'i 'od gsal rdo rje
5b5(1): snying po thun mong ma yin pa'i lung ltar 'chad pa'i dbang du byas na/ 'khor ba dang mya ngan 'das pa gnyis gang du'ang dbyer mi 'byed pa kun gyi sngon rol du srid zhi yongs la mnga'
5b6(1): dbang sgyur ba'i ston pa kun tu bzang po nyid dbyings rang byung gi ye shes bde bar gshegs pa'i snying po gdod ma'i gzhi las gzhi snang du shar ba'i skad cig la rang snang du ngo shes pas
6a1(1): sa dugs/ / marnam pa mo ga
6a2(1): ye shes su sangs rgyas pa ste/ rgyud bla ma las/ thog ma dbus mtha' med cing rnam dbyer med// gnyis med gsum bral dri med rnam rtog med// ces gsungs
6a3(1): pa dang / 'jam dpal sgyu 'phrul dra ba las kyang / rnam par rtog med lhun gyis grub// dus gsum sangs rgyas las byed pa// sangs rgyas thog ma tha ma med//
6a4(1): dang po'i sangs rgyas ris med pa// zhes so// de'ang don la med kyang 'khrul snang glo bur ba'i sgrib gnyis bag chags dang bcas pa rang ngo la yongs su dag pas spang ba chen
6a5(1): pa/ shes dang shes bya gnyis su med pa'i ye shes chen pos srid zhi ris su ma chad pa kun khyab tu gzigs pas rtogs pa chen po/ de dag gi mthus 'pho ba thams cad kyi
6a6(1): don dmigs pa med par rang bzhin lhun gyis grub pa'i phrin las mdzad pa ni sems chen po ste/ mngon rtogs rgyan las/ sems can kun mchog nyid sems dang /
6b1(1): grangs dang tshogs dang gsum po la// chen po gsum gyi rang byung gi/ ched du bya ba 'di shes bya// zhes so// de nyid ci yang mi dmigs pa smras pa'i mtha' thams cad dang bral
6b2(1): ba chos kyi dbyings kyi ye shes rang 'khor 'das bzang ngan med par mnyam pa nyid du gzigs pas srid zhi'i mtha' la mi gnas pa mnyam pa nyid kyi ye shes te ji la ba'i mkhyen pa'i ye
6b3(1): shes la dbang 'byor pas rgyu'i theg pa bdag gis 'jug pa thams cad chos kyi dbyings su zhi ba'i 'gog pa dam pa la gnas par bshad pa'i stong kyang tsam las 'das pa ste/ de bzhin
6b4(1): gshegs pa rnams kyi so so rang gi ye shes kyis gzigs pa'i yul sa bcu'i dbang phyug rgyal sras rnams dang / gdul bya'i tshogs la gzugs sku mig la snang ba dang / rna bar
6b5(1): gsung thos pa dang / 'phags pa'i tshul khrims kyi dri snom pa dang / chos kyi ro myong ba dang / ting nge 'dzin bde ba'i reg snang ba dang / rtog dpyod kyi shes rab kyis chos la
6b6(1): 'jal ba sogs kyi gzhi 'am rgyur gyur pa'i thim la ma rmugs pa'i ye shes phra ba'i rang bzhin nang gsal gzhon nu bum pa sku'i zhing khams chen por shel 'od nang du bsdus pa'i tshul can du
7a1(1): rgya kya na 'ang na na spyan pam rnam pa ma pas ma na na pa'i sam lapa yang brgyangam tshan
7a2(1): su ma lhungs par sangs rgyas nyid kyi ye shes kyis bsdus pa'i rang snang longs spyod rdzogs sku'i dkyil 'khor nges pa lnga ldan gyi bdag nyid can rigs lnga'i ston pa rnams kyang sku dang ye shes
7a3(1): tha mi dad kyi rol pa chen por bzhugs pa las dus gzhan du gdod ma'i gzhi las gzhi snang du shar ba'i rtsa la rang ngor ma shes pas rmi lam lta bu'i sems can rnams 'khrul pa'i rgyu med
7a4(1): bzhin la 'khrul pa ltar snang ba'i sdug bsngal gyi 'khor lo g.yo bar gzigs te/ brtse ba'i thugs rje skyes nas de dag gi don du zhing khams kyi bkod pa rgya chen po sprul pa ni rang snang
7a5(1): longs spyod rdzogs sku ye shes rigs lnga gang chen mtsho'i phyag rgya'i gnas rnams dang ba spu'i khung bu re re la'ang 'byung ba bzhi'i rdul phra rab ji snyed pa'i go thams cad na zhing khams
7a6(1): chen po dbyings dang tshad dang thog tha la sogs pa brjod pa'i yul thams cad las 'das pa kho nas rgyas par brtsams shing / de dag kyang rnam pa tha dad pa ste/ phan tshun
7b1(1): 'dres pa dang / rnam pa gzhan du skye zhing 'gyur ba dang / 'pho zhing ltung ba dang / rdzas gzhan gyis gos pa cung zad kyang med par zhing dang sku rgya mtshos chos kyi dbyings gang bar gyur pa
7b2(1): ste/ sdong po bkod pa'i mdo las/ sru yi rtse mo gcig la yang // zhing rnams bkod pa bsam mi khyab// sna tshogs dbyibs kyang tha dad de// de dag 'dres par gyur pa
7b3(1): med// ces dang / gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i mdo las/ zhi ba'i blo gros/ nam mkhas ci tsam khyab pa de tsam du// de bzhin gshegs pa'i zhing dang skus khyab bo//
7b4(1): zhes gsungs pa ltar/ de dag kyang sangs rgyas sku gsum gyi so so'i zhing khams mi 'dra ba gsum du bkod pa ni chos sku'i dus su 'od gsal rdo rje snying po'i zhing dang / rang
7b5(1): snang longs sku'i dus su tshangs pa rnga sgra'i zhing dang / sbrul sku'i dus su tshangs chen gyi bskal pa zhes bya la de dag rnams su gdod ma'i mgon po nyid kyi sprul pa'i sangs
7b6(1): rgyas rgya mtsho dus gsum du byon pa rnams dang / sems can gyi khams rgya mtsho yang yod de 'byung ba bzhi dang nam mkhas khyab tshad thams cad tshangs chen bskal pa
8a1(1): 'di'i khongs su 'dul/ der ma dag pa'i sems can rnams 'chi 'pho ba dang / skye zhing 'byung ba dang / sangs rgyas rnams mya ngan la 'da' ba dang
8a2(1): bstan pa gnas pa dang / nub pa dang / lam sgrub pa la sogs bde sdug gi snang ba sna tshogs la spyod pa'i tshul dang / de ltar rdul phran re re'i go na'ang ri gling rgya mtsho sogs
8a3(1): zhing khams tshad med pa snang zhing der ma zad rdul gcig gi steng gi 'jig rten de'i rdul phra ba gcig la'ang sems can gyi khams tshad med pa gnas pa rnams bde bar gshegs
8a4(1): pa'i rnam 'phrul dang / byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi zhing skyong ba'i smon lam gyi mthu chen po dang / sems can rnams kyi 'khrul snang gis las kyi tshogs mngon
8a5(1): par 'du bgyis pa dang / chos nyid kyis rab tu thob pa la sogs pa'i rgyu dang rkyen gyis rab tu tshogs pa ste/ sangs rgyas phal po che las/ sangs rgyas ye shes
8a6(1): yul ni bsam yas pas// byin rlab rnam 'phrul de dag 'di lta bu// zhing khams rgya mtsho bstan pa mtha' dbus med// rnam par snang mdzad chos kyis yongs su
8b1(1): sbyangs// byang chub sems ni kun gyi bsam pa bzhin// smon lam rgya mtsho bsam yas rnams sbyangs shing // sems can las rnams rgya mtsho bsam yas pas// phyogs kun zhing
8b2(1): rnams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung // byang chub sems dpa' kun gyi rnam 'phrul dang // thams cad mkhyen pa nyid la 'jug pa'i sgo// smon lam rgya mtsho thams cad mngon
8b3(1): bsgrubs shing // nam mkha'i dbyings la 'byams klas zhing 'byung ngo // spyod pa rgya mtshos mtha' dang dbus med rnams// spyod cing tshad med bder gshegs yul
8b4(1): la 'jug/ phyogs kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho kun byang zhing // bskal pa mtha' yas zhing rnams re rer skyong // sems can bsam dbyings bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i//
8b5(1): las kyi zhing rnams rgya mtsho thams cad 'byung // zhes dang / bzang po spyod pa las/ sgra tsam khyon la dus gsum tshad rnyed kyi// sangs rgyas rgya mtsho zhing rnams rgya
8b6(1): mtsho dang // smon lam rgya mtsho spyod cing rab tu 'jug/ ces so// de dag kyang don la med pa gsal snang yin te chos kyi dbyings la kun rdzob pa rnams gdod nas grub
9a1(1): ma myong ba'i phyir ro// gnyis pa de las zhing 'dir rdo rje 'chang gis sangs rgyas brnyes tshul ni// zhing 'di'i gdul bya'i don du thog ma'i sangs
9a2(1): rgyas kun tu bzang po nyid kyis thabs la mkhas pa'i rnam 'phrul chen pos so skye rang ga mas sems bskyed pa ltar bstan nas sangs rgyas pa'i tshul dang mdzad pa'i rol pa bkye
9a3(1): ba ste tshul de lta bu ni thun mong gi theg par yang grags te/ yab sras mjal ba'i mdo las// dpa' bo chen po thabs mkhas te// sems can yongs su smin bya'i
9a4(1): phyir// bye ba phrag brgyad rgyal ba nyid// sangs rgyas nyid du bstan gyur kyang // da dung du yang 'dren pa khyod// sangs rgyas mdzad pa mang ston mdzad// ces pa dang //
9a5(1): 'phags pa phal po che las/ byang chub rgya mtshor ba brnyes gyur nas kyang // sems can rgya mtsho rab tu smin bya'i phyir// byang chub sems bskyed rgya mtsho ston mdzad cing //
9a6(1): mi 'grib spyod pa rgya mtsho dus kun ston// bde gshegs rnams kyi rnam 'phrul de 'dra'o// zhes gsungs pa bzhin/ 'di nas bsal ba dpag tu med pa'i sngon rol du
9b1(1): zhing khams rang bzhin rnam par bkod pa zhes bya bar thog ma'i mgon po'i rnam par 'phrul pas sangs rgyas me tog mdzes pa chen po la gser gyi rdo rje gcig phul nas dang /
9b2(1): byang chub mchog tu thugs bskyed do// de nas skye ba gnyis nas khyim bdag legs sbyin gyi sras nor bu'i phreng ba zhes par gyur nas sangs rgyas 'khor lo legs par spyod pa
9b3(1): drung du chos mnyan/ de nas glog gi 'od ces bya ba'i sras bram ze'i khye'u legs byin ces par gyur te sangs rgyas dge ba'i blo gros la chos nyan cing lo bdun du ting nge 'dzin la
9b4(1): gnas shing / bdun cu rtsa lnga'i mthar gyis rin po che'i phung po rnam par bkod pa zhes bya ba'i ri bo'i rtse mor mngon par rdzogs pa sangs rgyas pa'i tshul bstan nas chos su'i
9b5(1): dgongs par bskal chen gcig tu bzhugs shing longs spyod thams cad rdzogs pa'i sru rgyan dang kha dog gi 'khor lor rang byon cing de nyid kyi ngang las rang snang gi rgyal ba rigs lnga
9b6(1): dkyil 'khor grangs las 'das pa rang byung la/ snang cha las mtshan dang dpe byad yongasasu rdzogs pa rdo rje 'chang gi skur byung ba ni thugs bskyed pI rten rdo rje phul ba las byung
10a1(1): / bar// dedas kyang rba// mang zugs mi zad pa can gyi 'amar lo'i mdzad pa sam cu rtswa drus la dbang 'byur pa mi slong thog gi 'chad rdul phyugs gcig
10a2(1): yin la/ don la gong du bshad pa ltar thog ma'i mgon po'i thabs la mkhas pa'i sgyu 'phrul tsam las tha mi dad cing gsang sngags kyi klung phal cher ston pa'i rdo rje 'chang dang
10a3(1): snying thig yang gsang gi rdo rje'i gnas zab mo ston pa la kun tu bzang po dang gzhan du dam pa dang po'i sangs rgyas dang / rdo rje sems dpa' sogs mtshan gyi rnam grangs du mas
10a4(1): bsnyad pa ste/ rtog bsdus las/ rab tu dag pa kun gyi mchog/ gdod nas grol ba de bzhin gshegs// kun tu bzang po kun gyi bdag/ byang chub sems nyid nges
10a5(1): pa'o// zhes dang / sems dpa' thog ma tha ma med// rdo rje sems dpa' dga' ba che// kun tu bzang po kun gyi bdag/ rdo rje snying po gtso ba'i gtso// gdod ma
10a6(1): tha ma med phyir yang // dam pa'i dang po zhes 'dod de// 'khor lo kun gyi gtso phyir na// dam pa dam pa'i dbang phyug yin// zhes gsungs pa ltar ro// gsum pa
10b1(1): gzugs sru la gnyis te/ longs sku dang sbrul sku'o// dang po ni/ sangs rgyas gsang ba'i lam rim las/ lhun rdzogs rig pa rang snang ba'i// zhing dang gzhal yas
10b2(1): gdan khri rgyan// 'od zer du mar snang ba ste// zhes bshad pa ltar chos kyi sku chen po nang gsal chos nyid kyi ngang du bzhugs pa de nyid man shel gyi nang 'od kha dog lnga nyi zer gyi
10b3(1): rkyen gyis gsal ba ltar rang snang gi yul la phyir gsal mched pa'i ye shes kyi snang cha sku dang zhing khams tshad med pa la longs su spyod pa'i gnas su sprul pa'i bkod pa rnam
10b4(1): bar snang mdzad gang chen mtsho'i phyag gi mthil na pad+ma'i sdong po skyes pa'i 'dab ma dang ze'u 'bru rnams la zhing khams nyi shu rtsa lnga re brtsegs mar gnas shing zhabs kyi skyil krung
10b5(1): man chad las spos chu'i rgyun 'bab pa dag tu'ang zhing khams bcu drug re yod pa de rnams su rigs lnga'i sangs rgyas nges pa lnga ldan gyi rang bzhin mtshan dang dpe byad rgya mtsho'i
10b6(1): bdag nyid rtag pa rgyun gyi 'khor lor longs spyod par grangs kyis mi lang bar bkod pa de dag ni ye shes gang chen mtsho'i zhing dang sku'i bkod pa longs sku chen po'i mtshan gzhi
11a1(1): ste de dag rdul gcig gi steng na rab 'byams rgya mtsho'i rdul snyed kyi zhing yang mi 'gal zhing sku gcig la rab 'byams rgya mtsho'i su 'du ba dang / sku re res
11a2(1): kyang rab 'byams rgya mtshor khyab pa sogs sgyu 'phrul rdo rje'i rol mo gsang ba bsam gyis mi khyab pa'i gnas su shes par bya ste/ gsang ba snying po las/ stong gsum yung
11a3(1): 'brur 'jug tshul gyis// dbyings nas dkyil 'khor spyan drang mchod// ces dang / phal po che las/ rdul gcig steng na rdul snyed sangs rgyas dang // ces sogs
11a4(1): gsungs pa bzhin no// zhing khams de dag la mnga' dbang mdzad pa'i ston pa longs spyod rdzogs pa'i sku de'ang rang bzhin bdun gyi khyad par dang ldan pa yin te/ de bzhin
11a5(1): nyid du nar son pa'i rang bzhin/ yon tan ma btsal bar lhun gyis grub pa'i rang bzhin/ ye shes mtha' dbus dang bral ba'i rang bzhin/ 'bras bu la mngar mdzad
11a6(1): kyang rang gi ngo bo bstan du med pa'i rang bzhin/ mnyam pa nyid mngon du mdzad kyang spyod yul dang bral ba'i rang bzhin/ gcig dang du ma las grol ba'i rang bzhin//
11b1(1): dus gsum 'du 'bral med pa'i rang bzhin te bdun gyi bdag nyid chen por lhun gyis grub pa nyid gdul bya'i dbang gis sku gsung thugs kyi mtshan ma sna tshogs par snang ba'i rnam
11b2(1): 'gyur gyi cha las mtshan dang dpe byad kyi rnam pa 'bar ba'i gzugs kyi sku la phyag zhabs 'khor los mtshan pa sogs mtshan bzang so gnyis dang / sen mo zangs mdog
11b3(1): sogs dpe byad brgyad cu rnams te thun mong gi mtshan dpe rnams dang / ston pa'i thugs ye shes bzhis phye ba'i rtsa la las phyi'i mtshan dpe/ rtsa 'khor rnams dag
11b4(1): pa'i cha las nang gi mtshan dpe/ khams byang chub kyi sems rnam par dag pa'i cha las gsang ba'i mtshan dpe ste longs spyod rdzogs pa chen po la rtsa khams rnam
11b5(1): bar dag pa bde ba chen po'i rang bzhin du ro mnyam pa ni rgyan gyi nang nas mdzes byed mchog tu gyur par bshad de/ sgyu 'phrul rgya mtsho las/ a li ka li bde ba
11b6(1): gnyis// phan tshun ma 'dres gcig par shes// bcu drug ngos gnyis mtshan dang ldan// phyogs gcig ye shes lnga ldan pa// brgyad cu'o bzod sogs rgyu las
12a1(1): 'phags// zhes so// rtog tshogs las shin tu 'das pa'i zag pa dang bral ba'i rnam par grol ba'i ye shes gzigs pa'i phung po dang /

12a3(1): yon tan phrin las lnga'i bdag nyid chen po rnam snang / mi bskyod/ rin 'byung / snang mtha'/ don grub lnga dang / khams lnga yang / dbyings
12a4(1): phyug// spyan ma/ mA ma kI/ gos dkar mo/ dam tshig sgrol mar rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pas mi 'gyur ba'i bde ba chen po dang rnam kun mchog ldan gyi
12a5(1): stong pa nyid la sbyor du bzhugs pa las/ dkyil dang / 'khor dang / so so'i tshom bu dang / yab dang / sam dang / sgyu mdog dang / phyag mtshan chags
12a6(1): can/ chags bral/ de bzhin gshegs pa/ gshegs ma/ sems dpa'/ sems ma/ khro bo/ khro mo sogs rol pa rmad du byung ba'i 'khor

12b2(1): bzhin/ sa snying / phyag rdor/ nam snying / spyan gzigs bzhi dang / yul gzugs sgra dri ro bzhi yang / sems ma sgeg mo/ phreng ba ma/ glu ma/ gar
12b3(1): ma bzhi dang / de bzhin du spyan dang / snyan dang / shangs dang / ljags te/ dbang po bzhi yang / byams pa/ sgrib sel/ kun bzang / 'jam dpal

12b5(1): btsun mo dang snyoms par 'jug pa'i gsang ba'i yul dbang rnam shes gsum 'dus kyi reg pa dang / reg byed/ reg bya/ reg shes kyis dga' ba chen po'i ro nyams
12b6(1): su myong ba yang mthar byed kyi khro bo chen po bzhi dang / rtag chad bdag mtshan bzhi yang khro mo chen mo bzhi'i rang bzhin dang ldan pa sogs mtha' yas pa'i 'khor gyi
13a1(1): sa byung na patshad myu ma rnas pa can la la rnas pa sa sa \u0f7f/
13a2(1): rgyud las/ rang rig mtha' dbus med pa'i dkyil// ye shes bzhi 'gro 'khor lo'i tshul// zhes dang / khog gzhung las/ 'bras bu mthar phyir 'og min na//
13a3(1): bzhug pa dkyil dang 'khor gyi tshul// zhes bshad pa ltar dang // de dag kyang sangs rgyas rang snang gi ye shes rnam pa thams cad pa'i bdag nyid sgyu 'phrul dra ba'i rol pa rnam pa kun tu zhing
13a4(1): dang / kun tu gdan dang / kun tu gzhal med khang dang / kun tu shar dang / kun tu steng dang / kun tu 'og dang / kun tu zlum po/ kun tu gru bzhi/ kun tu gru

13a6(1): ste ye shes kyi rtsal 'gag pa med pas chos kyi dbyings mtha' klas par khyab gdal ba'i phyir te/ seng ge rtsal rdzogs las/ kun tu bzang po'i zhal ni phyogs

13b3(1): ltar ro// sangs rgyas kyi yul de ni sangs rgyas kho na'i rgyud kyis bsdus pa'i phyir sa bcu'i dbang phyug rnams kyis kyang mi mthong ste/ sgrib pa mtha' dag las ma grol
13b4(1): zhing ji lta ba dang ji snyed pa mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi spyan rdul dang bral ba ma brnyes pa'i phyir te/ theg pa chen po'i bstan bcos rgyud bla ma las/ ngag yul min phyir
13b5(1): don dam gyis bsdus phyir// rtogs gnas min phyir dpe las 'das phyir dang // bla na med phyir srid zhis ma bsdus phyir// rgyal sum 'phags rnams kyis kyang bsre
13b6(1): mi khyab// ces gsungs pa ltar ro// gang du 'jig rten las 'das pa'i zhing khams phun sum tshogs pa de rnams kyang rang snang gzhi'i 'od gsal chen po'i snang cha
14a1(1): dag pa rab 'byams kyi 'khang lar snod bcung du shar ba rmi lam dag pa dang chos mtshungs pas gang gi tshe gzung 'dzin bag chags cha bcas rnam par byung

14a3(1): rang rig blo med na// bde chen zhing yang ngan song gnas su mthong // theg mchog mnyam pa'i don nyid rtogs pa na// ngan song gnas kyang 'og min dga' ldan gnas// /
14a4(1): zhes gsungs pa bzhin no// gnyis pa sprul pa'i sku la'ang gsum ste/ rang bzhin sprul pa/ 'gro 'dul sprul pa/ sna tshogs sprul pa'o// de yang gdul bya rang
14a5(1): rgyud kyi bder gshegs snying po la sgrib byed kyi dri ma ma dag pa dang / cung zad dag pa/ shin tu dag pa gsum gyi go rim la ltos nas 'dul byed kyi ston pa yang de ltar
14a6(1): snang ba yin te shin tu dag pa chos kyi sku la 'khor 'das ro mnyam chen po nyid kyi phyir don dam pa'i dbyings las ma g.yos bzhin du gzugs kyi sku ni rtsol ba med pa'i
14b1(1): thugs rje chen po'i rnam 'phrul 'gag pa med pa'i rol pa ci yang bkye ba las gdul bya 'dul byed gnyis ltar snang ba'i gzhan dbang gi tshul du mos pa'i chu snong
14b2(1): rnyog pa med pa ji snyed du sprul pa'i zla gzugs de snyed 'char ba chos nyid de/ rje btsun gyis/ ji ltar bai DUr sa gzhi gtsang ma la// lha dbang lus kyi gzugs
14b3(1): brnyan snang ba ltar// de bzhin 'gro sems sa gzhi gtsang ma la// thub pa'i dbang po'i sku yi gzugs brlan 'char// zhes dang / mdo las/ rgyal ba'i chos
14b4(1): nyid lus med rab zhi pa// gnyis med rang bzhin med par thugs chud nas// gzugs su bzang po mtshan gyis brgyan pa yis// 'gro ba ma lus bkang zhing stan
14b5(1): par mdzad// ces gsungs pa ltar ro// de la rang bzhin sprul pa ni gong gi dbyings snang longs sku chen po'i ston pa de nyid ji ltar dwangs shel la gzugs brlan 'phos pa
14b6(1): ltar cung zad dag pa'i gdul bya sa bcu'i dbang phyug rnams la snang ba ni 'di ltar rang bzhin sbrul sku'i zhing khams dbus na 'og min dang / phyogs bzhir rim pa
15a1(1): na man pa du/ sa pa gas pa labar 'dzums ldan pa ni bzhin gaganas pa garnams sarnal

22a1(1): stong rtsa gcig/ bstan pa kun gyi rtsa ba sgra thal 'gyur/ sdud pa po lha'i bu dga' byed dbang phyug/ grogs lha'i bu nyi ma rab tu snang byed//
22a2(1): sems can rnams tshe lo dpag tu med pa thub pa'i dus na'o// gnas 'jig rten mi mjed du/ ston pa khye'u 'od mi 'khrugs pa/ 'khor mkha' gro ma 'bum phrag
22a3(1): gnyis/ bstan pa sku gsung thugs yon tan phrin las kyi rgyud lnga dus tshe lo bye ba'i dus na'o// gnas drod gsher 'dus pa 'od kyis srungs par ston pa dpal 'jigs

22b3(1): bdun/ chos pha rgyud ma rgyud la sogs pa rgyud sde du ma dang / dus tshe lo drug khri'i dus su'o// gnas srin phug ru lu'i sgra dang ldan par/ ston pa drang srong

58b2(1): stong pa nyid du blta ba ni de lta ma yin no// de ci'i phyir zhe na/ 'od srung lta bar gyur pa thams cad las 'byung ba ni stong pa nyid yin na 'od srung gang stong pa nyid kho nar blta/
